17.2 State Management
typescript// Utiliser Zustand (simple) ou Redux Toolkit (complexe)

// store/draftsStore.ts
import create from 'zustand';

interface DraftsState {
  drafts: Draft[];
  selectedDrafts: string[];
  filters: Filters;
  
  setDrafts: (drafts: Draft[]) => void;
  addDraft: (draft: Draft) => void;
  updateDraft: (id: string, data: Partial<Draft>) => void;
  deleteDraft: (id: string) => void;
  
  toggleSelectDraft: (id: string) => void;
  selectAllDrafts: () => void;
  clearSelection: () => void;
  
  setFilters: (filters: Partial<Filters>) => void;
}

export const useDraftsStore = create<DraftsState>((set) => ({
  drafts: [],
  selectedDrafts: [],
  filters: {},
  
  setDrafts: (drafts) => set({ drafts }),
  addDraft: (draft) => set((state) => ({ 
    drafts: [...state.drafts, draft] 
  })),
  // ... autres mÃ©thodes
}));
17.3 API Client
typescript// lib/api.ts
import axios from 'axios';

const api = axios.create({
  baseURL: process.env.REACT_APP_API_URL || 'http://localhost:8000',
  timeout: 30000,
});

// Interceptor pour auth
api.interceptors.request.use((config) => {
  const token = localStorage.getItem('token');
  if (token) {
    config.headers.Authorization = `Bearer ${token}`;
  }
  return config;
});

// Interceptor pour errors
api.interceptors.response.use(
  (response) => response,
  (error) => {
    if (error.response?.status === 401) {
      // Redirect to login
      window.location.href = '/login';
    }
    return Promise.reject(error);
  }
);

// API methods
export const draftsAPI = {
  getAll: () => api.get('/drafts'),
  getById: (id: string) => api.get(`/drafts/${id}`),
  create: (data: CreateDraftData) => api.post('/drafts', data),
  update: (id: string, data: UpdateDraftData) => 
    api.patch(`/drafts/${id}`, data),
  delete: (id: string) => api.delete(`/drafts/${id}`),
  bulkPublish: (ids: string[]) => 
    api.post('/drafts/bulk-publish', { ids }),
};

export default api;
```

  --font-display: 'Cal Sans', 'Inter', sans-serif; /* Pour titres hero */
}

/* Scale typographique harmonieuse (systÃ¨me 1.25) */
--text-xs: 0.75rem;    /* 12px - Captions, labels */
--text-sm: 0.875rem;   /* 14px - Body small, secondary */
--text-base: 1rem;     /* 16px - Body principal */
--text-lg: 1.125rem;   /* 18px - Emphasis */
--text-xl: 1.25rem;    /* 20px - H3 */
--text-2xl: 1.5rem;    /* 24px - H2 */
--text-3xl: 1.875rem;  /* 30px - H1 */
--text-4xl: 2.25rem;   /* 36px - Hero */
Spacing cohÃ©rent (systÃ¨me 4px)
css--space-1: 0.25rem;  /* 4px */
--space-2: 0.5rem;   /* 8px */
--space-3: 0.75rem;  /* 12px */
--space-4: 1rem;     /* 16px - Base */
--space-6: 1.5rem;   /* 24px */
--space-8: 2rem;     /* 32px */
--space-12: 3rem;    /* 48px */
--space-16: 4rem;    /* 64px */
```

### Design specs Messagerie
```
Conversations List :
- Width : 320px fixe
- Item padding : 16px
- Border-bottom : 1px solid var(--border-light)
- Active item : Background var(--primary-50), border-left 3px primary
- Badge non-lu : Blue dot 8px, position absolute
- Hover : Background var(--surface-1)
- Avatar : 40px, border-radius full
- Truncate texte : 2 lignes max avec ellipsis
- Timestamp : 11px, tertiary, align right

Conversation Area :
- Padding : 24px
- Messages : 
  - Sent (vous) : align right, background primary-100, border-radius lg
  - Received : align left, background surface-2, border-radius lg
  - Max-width : 70%
  - Padding : 12px 16px
  - Margin between : 8px
  - Timestamp : 11px, tertiary, en-dessous

Input Area :
- Border-top : 1px solid border-light
- Padding : 16px
- Background : surface-0
- Textarea : Auto-grow, max 5 lignes
- Boutons : Icon buttons 36x36px
```

css/* Primary Button */
.btn-primary {
  background: var(--primary-500);
  color: white;
  padding: 10px 20px; /* Medium */

  font-weight: 500;
  transition: all 0.2s ease;
}

  background: var(--primary-600);
  transform: translateY(-1px);
  box-shadow: var(--shadow-md);
}

/* Sizes */

.btn-md { padding: 10px 20px; font-size: 14px; }
.btn-lg { padding: 12px 24px; font-size: 16px; }

.btn-outline { border: 1px solid var(--border-medium); background: transparent; }

.btn-danger { background: var(--error); color: white; }

    left: 100%;
  }
